## 2) Canonical runtime modes & pipelines

### Mode: Research/Training
Static mode inferred from training modules and CLI entrypoints. Starts from ingest/providers, builds datasets/features, trains models, writes manifests/artifacts. Unknown from static read for scheduler details.

### Mode: Evaluation/Backtest
Static mode inferred from eval/promotion/validation modules and run manifests. Replays model outputs against held-out periods and computes promotion metrics. Unknown from static read for full runtime flags.

### Mode: Paper/Live Execution
Static mode inferred from execution/trading modules and cooc sleeve execution scripts. Translates signals to orders with risk/constraint layers and emits telemetry.

### Mode: Frontend observability
Vite/Next UI pages consume API/SSE and render run dashboards and artifacts.

## 7) Final deliverable summary

### Top 10 architectural strengths
1. Modular domain partitioning across `algaie`, `backend`, `sleeves`, and `frontend`.
2. Presence of dedicated pipeline modules for ingest/canonicalize/train/validate/export.
3. Explicit test directories in multiple subsystems.
4. Config-driven setup via YAML/TOML/JSON manifests.
5. Separation of UI and backend services.
6. Artifact-oriented workflow with run folders and manifests.
7. Domain-specific sleeves abstraction for strategy isolation.
8. Validation and promotion modules indicate gated model lifecycle.
9. Provider abstraction hints for data-source swapping.
10. Rich docs footprint indicating operational awareness.
### Top 10 architectural risks
1. Large repository with mixed active/deprecated code increases drift risk.
2. Entrypoint sprawl across scripts/CLIs can reduce operator clarity.
3. Heavily file-based artifacts may lack centralized metadata guarantees.
4. Potential duplicated logic across backend/algaie/sleeves layers.
5. Unknown static guarantees for retries/idempotency in execution path.
6. Cross-language API contracts may not be strongly typed end-to-end.
7. Config fragmentation may cause inconsistent runtime behavior.
8. Potential performance bottlenecks in parquet-heavy transformations.
9. Secrets/auth posture not obvious from static scan.
10. Test-to-module traceability is incomplete without explicit mapping.
### 90-day refactor roadmap (phased, minimal breaking changes)
1. **Days 1-30:** inventory & deprecate map; formalize entrypoint matrix; add module owners and CI checks.
2. **Days 31-60:** unify config schema/version hashing; introduce artifact catalog index; standardize telemetry envelope.
3. **Days 61-90:** consolidate duplicate pipeline logic; harden execution retries/guards; expand contract tests across UI/API/pipelines.
